### [158] [Robotic Policy Adaptation via Weight-Space Meta-Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07217)
*Christian Bianchi,Siamak Yousefi,Alessio Sampieri,Andrea Roberti,Luca Rigazio,Fabio Galasso,Luca Franco*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: WIZARD是一种权重空间元学习框架，通过单次前向传播为目标VLA策略生成任务特定的LoRA参数，避免了对新任务进行微调、动作标签或测试时优化，在LIBERO和Franka Emika Panda上实现了显著性能提升。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有的VLA模型在适应新任务时通常需要任务特定的演示数据、动作标注和额外微调，部署成本高且难以规模化扩展。作者希望摆脱这种对任务特定数据和高成本微调的依赖。

Method: 提出WIZARD框架：基于权重空间元学习，给定语言指令和短视频演示，在单次前向传播中预测出对应的任务特定LoRA参数，直接应用于冻结的VLA策略，无需目标任务的动作标签或测试时优化。元训练阶段学习从任务证据映射到专家LoRA更新的映射关系。

Result: 在LIBERO数据集上，WIZARD在未见数据集集合上性能提升约2倍，在未见任务上性能提升约14倍。在Franka Emika Panda真实机器人上，WIZARD持续优于真实域适配基线，表明生成的适配器能够提供超越仿真环境的任务级专门化。

Conclusion: WIZARD通过权重空间元学习高效生成任务特定适配器，显著降低VLA策略适应新任务的数据成本和计算开销，同时展示了在仿真和真实场景中的泛化能力。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models are emerging as a promising paradigm for robotic manipulation, enabling general-purpose policies trained from large corpora of demonstrations and action labels. However, adapting these models to new tasks still typically requires task-specific demonstrations, action annotations, and additional fine-tuning, making deployment costly and difficult to scale.
  We propose WIZARD, a weight-space meta-learning framework that sidesteps task-specific fine-tuning by generating task-specific LoRA parameters for a frozen VLA policy. Given only a language instruction and a short demonstration video, WIZARD predicts the corresponding adaptation weights in a single forward pass, without target-task action labels or test-time optimization. During meta-training, WIZARD learns to map task evidence directly to expert LoRA updates, capturing relationships between tasks in weight space.
  Experiments on LIBERO show that WIZARD improves performance by up to ~2x on unseen dataset collections and up to ~14x on unseen tasks. On a Franka Emika Panda, WIZARD consistently improves over a real-domain adapted baseline, showing that generated adapters provide task-level specialization beyond simulation.

</details>


### [159] [RhinoVLA Technical Report](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07383)
*Huixi Intelligence,:,Chen Zhang,Chenyang Zhou,Guanglei Ding,Guanghui He,Haibin Gao,Jiajia Chen,Jianyong Zhang,Lianyi Yu,Ningyi Xu,Ping Xu,Qingchen Li,Yingjun Hu,Yijia Zhang,Yuxi Liu*

Main category: cs.RO

TL;DR: 本文提出RhinoVLA，一种部署导向的VLA模型，通过与Huixi R1边缘SoC协同设计，解决视觉-语言-动作模型在边缘硬件上的实时部署延迟问题。通过采用token高效的Qwen3-VL骨干网络、连续动作专家、统一跨机器人接口以及硬件感知编译优化，在保持与π0.5相当性能的同时，在Huixi R1上实现了11.69 Hz的端到端推理，满足10 Hz实时闭环控制需求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VLA模型在边缘硬件上实时部署存在严重的延迟瓶颈，其中VLM的视觉和上下文token在GEMM主导的投影算子中导致计算量随token数线性增长，限制了机器人实时闭环控制（10 Hz目标）的实现。

Method: 1) 采用token高效的Qwen3-VL骨干网络减少VLM侧token和计算负担；2) 引入连续Action Expert保持预训练多模态能力；3) 提出统一接口（View Registry、72D物理状态-动作槽空间、机器人实例LoRA）支持跨异构机器人学习；4) 通过硬件感知编译、混合精度执行和并行视觉编码进行部署优化。

Result: RhinoVLA在相似参数规模下达到与π0.5相当的下游任务性能，在Huixi R1芯片上实现11.69 Hz的端到端推理，超过了10 Hz的实时闭环控制目标。

Conclusion: 通过模型-硬件协同设计和token效率优化，VLA模型可以在边缘设备上实现实时部署，且不牺牲任务性能。该项目将开源。

Abstract: Vision-Language-Action (VLA) models have shown strong potential for robotic manipulation, but real-time deployment on edge hardware remains challenging. In this work, we identify VLM visual and context tokens as a major source of deployment latency: for GEMM-dominated projection operators, computation grows linearly with the number of input tokens when model dimensions are fixed. Motivated by this observation, we propose RhinoVLA, a deployment-oriented VLA model co-designed with the Huixi R1 edge SoC. RhinoVLA adopts a token-efficient Qwen3-VL backbone and a continuous Action Expert, reducing the VLM-side token and computation burden while preserving pretrained multimodal capability. To support cross-robot learning, RhinoVLA further introduces a unified interface that combines View Registry, 72D physical state-action slot space, and robotinstance LoRA, allowing heterogeneous robot observations and action schemas to be aligned under a shared policy. On the deployment side, RhinoVLA is optimized through hardware-aware compilation, mixed-precision execution, and parallel visual encoding. Experiments show that RhinoVLA achieves downstream performance comparable to π0.5 at a similar parameter scale, while reaching 11.69 Hz end-to-end inference on Huixi R1, meeting the 10 Hz real-time closedloop control target. The project will be open-sourced at https://github.com/HuixiAI/RhinoVLA.

</details>

### [160] [Deployed trusted-node quantum key distribution over 300 km with a multi-core fiber access link](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06107)
*Martin Clason,Joakim Argillander,Didrik Bergström,Daniel Spegel-Lexne,Giulio Foletto,Ashraf El Hassan,Mohamed Bourennane,Onur Günlü,Katia Gallo,Rui Lin,Guilherme B. Xavier*

TL;DR: 在瑞典国家量子通信基础设施中，通过270公里单模光纤加33公里多芯光纤（总303公里）实现了可信节点量子密钥分发（QKD），使用商业QKD系统与外部超导纳米线单光子探测器，成功在经典流量共存和动态芯切换条件下运行。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将QKD部署到现实通信网络中面临长距离、异质光纤基础设施以及与经典流量共存等挑战，需要验证商业QKD系统在苛刻、动态可重构光纤基础设施中的可行性。

Method: 使用商业QKD系统，接收器外接超导纳米线单光子探测器以支持更高损耗；在270公里单模光纤+33公里多芯光纤（MCF）段上运行；主动切换QKD通道在两个MCF纤芯之间，同时其他纤芯传输以太网流量和注入宽带光学噪声。

Result: 成功在303公里总距离上实现QKD运行，支持动态纤芯切换和经典流量共存，验证了商业QKD在现实复杂光纤基础设施中的集成能力。

Conclusion: 商业QKD可集成到苛刻的动态可重构光纤网络中；但QKD生成密钥的有限性和时变性会显著影响基于一次性密钥加密的图像传输保真度，揭示了实际场景中QKD加密面临的应用层挑战。

Abstract: Quantum key distribution (QKD) is increasingly considered for deployment in realistic communication networks, where long distances, heterogeneous fiber infrastructure, and coexistence with classical traffic present substantial challenges. Here, we demonstrate trusted-node QKD between Linköping University and the Stockholm hub of the Swedish national quantum communication infrastructure over 270 km of deployed single-mode fiber, extended by a 33 km multi-core fiber (MCF) segment emulating a metropolitan access link, for a total distance of 303 km. The two sub-links use commercial QKD systems whose receivers are interfaced with external superconducting nanowire single-photon detectors, enabling operation at losses beyond those supported by standard internal gated-mode detectors. We operate the link while actively switching the QKD channel between two MCF cores, with co-propagating Ethernet traffic and injected broadband optical noise in the other cores. The results demonstrate the integration of commercial QKD into demanding, dynamically reconfigurable fiber infrastructure relevant to future hybrid quantum-classical networks. Finally, using the generated secret keys, we illustrate how limited and time-varying QKD throughput affects one-time-pad-protected image transmission: image fidelity depends strongly on the available QKD-generated key budget and the choice of compression algorithm, highlighting application-level challenges for QKD-based encryption in realistic scenarios.

### [161] [Phonetic Error Analysis of Raw Waveform Acoustic Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07030)
*Erfan Loweimi,Zhengjun Yue,Andrea Carmantini,Zoran Cvetkovic,Steve Renals,Peter Bell*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文对TIMIT音素识别任务中原始波形声学模型的错误模式进行了深入分析，超越了仅关注整体音素错误率(PER)的局限。模型结合参数化(SincNet, Sinc2Net)或非参数化CNN与双向LSTM，在Dev/Test上分别达到13.9%/15.3%的PER，是原始波形模型在TIMIT上的最佳结果。通过WSJ迁移学习，PER进一步降至11.3%/12.3%，超越了Filterbank基线。每BPC分析显示：BLSTM层对过渡依赖类别的提升最大，而WSJ迁移学习对辅音的改善约比元音高三倍。混淆模式在各系统间保持一致，表明主导混淆反映了固有的语音相似性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注原始波形模型在TIMIT音素识别上的整体PER，忽视了模型在不同语音类别上的具体表现差异。本文旨在通过更细致的错误分析（按三大语音类别分解、混淆矩阵分析）来揭示原始波形模型的错误模式。

Method: 使用参数化(SincNet, Sinc2Net)或非参数化CNN结合双向LSTM构建原始波形声学模型；在TIMIT数据集上进行音素识别；通过WSJ进行迁移学习；将PER按三大语音类别(BPC)分解，并从替换错误构建混淆矩阵进行详细分析。

Result: 原始波形模型在TIMIT Dev/Test上达到13.9%/15.3%的PER，为当时最佳；WSJ迁移学习将PER降至11.3%/12.3%，超越Filterbank基线；BLSTM层对过渡依赖类别提升最明显；WSJ迁移学习改善辅音的效果是元音的三倍；混淆模式在各系统间一致，反映固有语音相似性。

Conclusion: 原始波形模型在TIMIT音素识别上可达到甚至超越传统Filterbank基线；不同模型组件对不同语音类别的影响存在显著差异；混淆模式的跨系统一致性表明其源于语音本身的固有特性。

Abstract: We analyse error patterns of raw waveform acoustic models on TIMIT phone recognition beyond the overall phone error rate (PER). PER is decomposed across three broad phonetic class (BPC) categorisations, and confusion matrices are constructed from substitution errors. Our models combine parametric (SincNet, Sinc2Net) or non-parametric CNNs with Bidirectional LSTMs, achieving 13.9%/15.3% PER on Dev/Test, the best reported results for raw waveform models on TIMIT. Transfer learning from WSJ reduces PER to 11.3%/12.3%, surpassing the Filterbank baseline. Per-BPC analysis reveals that BLSTM layers benefit transition-dependent classes most, while WSJ transfer learning improves consonants roughly three times more than vowels. Confusion patterns are consistent across raw waveform and Filterbank systems, indicating that the dominant confusions reflect inherent phonetic similarities.

### [162] [Entropy as a Structural Prior: How a Log-Barrier on DiT Belief Space Drives Musical Diversity and Development](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07207)
*Zixi Li,Youzhen Li*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文提出Eisbach对数障碍函数，利用DiT输出空间能量分布的熵作为置信度权重，在监督扩散训练中避免了传统置信度加权导致错误加速的问题，应用于Stable Audio 3的LoRA微调后意外提升了音质和多样性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统观点认为生成模型中应避免基于置信度的损失加权，因为模型自信错误时会加速错误传播。但作者发现监督扩散训练中这一直觉不成立，因此探索利用输出熵作为自适应权重的方法。

Method: 提出Eisbach对数障碍函数：根据DiT输出空间能量分布的熵计算无参数权重——高熵抑制梯度，低熵保留梯度。将该方法应用于Stable Audio 3 Medium在MusicCaps上的LoRA微调。

Result: 相比无权重训练，该方法意外地产生了更强的主题发展、更清晰的声学区分和更高的纹理多样性，与模式坍缩相反。验证了监督扩散中梯度方向锚定真实值，置信度仅缩放步长；时间熵抑制平坦样本而保留高对比度样本。

Conclusion: 该方法形成了一种在线、自我参考的数据课程，完全源自前向传播。提供了噪声级动力学分析和可检验的预测。

Abstract: Confidence-based loss weighting is usually avoided in generative models because it accelerates errors when the model is confidently wrong, but this intuition breaks down in supervised diffusion training. We introduce the Eisbach log-barrier, a parameter-free weight derived from the entropy of the DiT output's spatial energy distribution: high entropy damps the gradient, while low entropy preserves it. Applied to LoRA fine-tuning of Stable Audio 3 Medium on MusicCaps, it unexpectedly yields stronger thematic development, clearer acoustic differentiation, and higher textural diversity than unweighted training, the opposite of mode collapse. This works because in supervised diffusion the gradient direction is locked to ground truth, so confidence only scales the step size, and because temporal entropy downweights flat samples while preserving high-contrast ones. The result is an online, self-referential data curriculum that emerges purely from the forward pass, with analyzed noise-level dynamics and testable predictions.

</details>


### [163] [TargetSEC: Plug-and-Play In-the-Wild Speech Emotion Conversion via Arousal-Conditioned Latent Style Diffusion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07293)
*Constantin Alexander Auga*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: TargetSEC是一个基于嵌入驱动的潜在扩散框架，用于语音情感转换。它在紧凑的潜在空间中生成以情感为中心的风格嵌入，条件依赖于说话人身份和连续情感，在MSP-Podcast数据集上实现了高转换准确率和高语音质量。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有固定时长的语音情感转换方法存在两难：要么高语音质量但情感转换效果差，要么转换效果好但语音自然度下降。作者希望在不牺牲语音质量的前提下实现准确的情感转换。

Method: 提出TargetSEC框架，采用嵌入驱动的潜在扩散模型。核心思路是：在紧凑的潜在空间中生成以情感为中心的风格嵌入，以说话人身份和连续情感为条件进行扩散，而非直接在声谱图上做扩散。

Result: 在MSP-Podcast数据集上，TargetSEC在转换准确率上优于当前非时长基线方法，同时保持高语音质量；其性能与显式时长预测系统相当。

Conclusion: TargetSEC验证了潜在扩散框架在非平行、真实场景语音情感转换任务上的有效性，无需显式时长建模即可达到与时长预测系统可比的性能，为in-the-wild SEC任务提供了新的解决思路。

Abstract: Speech Emotion Conversion (SEC) aims to transform the emotion of a source utterance into a target emotion while preserving content and speaker identity. SEC on in-the-wild data is challenging due to the non-parallel nature of training data and complex real-world acoustics. Existing fixed-duration approaches either struggle to shift the emotion effectively (high quality, low conversion) or degrade speech naturalness (low quality, high conversion). We propose TargetSEC, an embedding-driven latent diffusion framework that generates emotion-focused style embeddings conditioned on speaker identity and continuous emotion. Unlike methods that diffuse over spectrograms, TargetSEC operates in a compact latent space. Experiments on the MSP-Podcast dataset show that TargetSEC outperforms current non-duration baselines in conversion accuracy while maintaining high speech quality, and achieves performance comparable to duration-prediction systems without explicit temporal modeling.

### [164] [How Far Can Chord-Symbol Time-Series Adaptation Carry Genre Identity? Capabilities and Boundaries in Multi-Genre Chord-Symbol Modeling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07334)
*Jinju Lee*

Main category: cs.SD

TL;DR: 本文研究在冻结的流行-爵士音乐Transformer上，通过LoRA、IA3、BitFit、prefix tuning和全微调五种轻量级适配方法，将模型扩展到11种目标音乐体裁的和弦符号序列建模。实验表明所有方法均优于冻结基线，LoRA和IA3表现最佳，但统计检验无显著差异。进一步分析发现IA3在数据量均衡时更优，而LoRA的优势部分源于数据量。错误体裁适配器也表现良好，说明轻量条件化比特定适配器更重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在小规模适配接口下，如何将预训练的和弦符号模型高效扩展到多样的音乐体裁，评估不同参数高效微调方法在音乐领域跨体裁迁移的效果。

Method: 基于冻结的pop-jazz Music Transformer，使用LoRA、IA3、BitFit、prefix tuning和全微调五种方法，在11种体裁（蓝调、波萨诺瓦、巴赫众赞歌、乡村、电子、民谣、放克、福音、嘻哈、R&B/灵魂、摇滚）上进行和弦序列预测，采用3个随机种子，共165格实验网格。还包括数据量控制实验、控制token基线、秩扫描、错误体裁旋转、消融实验等诊断分析。

Result: 所有五种适配方法在保留集和弦预测上均优于冻结基线，宏观增益+2.89至+3.61分。LoRA和IA3得分最高，但Wilcoxon检验（Holm和Benjamini-Hochberg校正）不支持显著胜出。数据量均衡后IA3保持领先，LoRA降至末位。错误体裁适配器也优于冻结基线。

Conclusion: 和弦符号适配确实能可靠提升体裁局部和声预测，但和弦符号本身并不完整承载体裁身份。结论有限：不涉及体裁真实性感知或完整音乐质量，这些需要受控的听众或音乐家评估。

Abstract: Harmony is a compact symbolic layer where mathematical pitch relations, acoustic consonance, and musical convention meet. This report treats chord-symbol sequences not as a complete representation of music, but as an interpretable, controllable time series for genre-local harmonic modeling. Starting from a frozen pop-jazz Music Transformer checkpoint, I evaluate how far small adaptation interfaces can extend the model to eleven target genres: blues, bossa nova, Bach chorales, country, electronic, folk, funk, gospel, hip-hop, R&B/soul, and rock. The main evaluation compares LoRA, IA3, BitFit, prefix tuning, and full fine-tuning over 11 genres and 3 seeds, a complete 165-cell grid. All five methods improve over the frozen base on held-out chord prediction, with macro gains from +2.89 to +3.61 points; LoRA and IA3 score highest, but Wilcoxon tests with Holm and Benjamini-Hochberg correction do not support a decisive winner. A matched-data-size control sharpens this: when genres are sub-sampled to a common corpus size, IA3 stays on top but LoRA's full-data edge disappears and it falls to last, indicating the small gaps are partly data-driven. A control-token baseline is also strong, and wrong-genre adapters often beat the frozen base, suggesting much of the effect comes from lightweight conditioning over a reusable harmonic base rather than one particular adapter family. Additional diagnostics (rank sweeps, wrong-genre rotation, a base-checkpoint ablation, chord-only genre classification, generated-output statistics, real-song evaluation, and duplicate analysis) support a bounded conclusion: chord-symbol adaptation reliably improves genre-local harmonic prediction, but chord symbols alone do not carry complete genre identity. The report therefore avoids claims about perceived genre authenticity or full musical quality, which require controlled listener or musician evaluation.

### [165] [Adjacency Spectral Radius Under Laplacian Sparsification: Deterministic and Probabilistic Bounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07459)
*Joshua Steier*

Main category: math.CO

TL;DR: 本文研究图谱稀疏化对邻接谱半径的影响，证明其可被（1±ε）控制，并针对重加权稀疏化、有效电阻采样等不同场景给出了确定性、高概率和基于特征向量离域化的误差界，最后通过下界证明正则图上的紧致性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Spielman-Srivastava谱稀疏化可保持Laplacian二次型在(1±ε)范围内，但无法直接控制邻接谱半径λ₁，而λ₁在NIMFA流行病阈值和谱聚类中至关重要，因此需要建立稀疏化后邻接谱半径的误差界。

Method: 1) 确定性证明：|λ₁(A_H)-λ₁(A_G)| ≤ ε(2Δ-λ₁)；2) 基于Perron-Frobenius单调性给出重加权稀疏化的ε·λ₁紧界；3) 有效电阻采样下，用Matrix Bernstein得到O(εΔ/√c)的高概率界；4) 结合特征向量离域化与预解摄动理论，对具有离域化Perron特征向量和谱间隙Ω(Δ)的图建立O(εΔ√(log n)/√n)+O(ε²Δ²/δ_gap)的误差界；5) 对Erdos-Renyi图、正则扩展图和随机块模型给出推论；6) 通过下界证明正则图上的紧致性。

Result: 建立了邻接谱半径在谱稀疏化下的多种误差界，包括确定性界、概率界和基于特征向量结构的界，并证明正则图下界的紧致性。

Conclusion: 本文系统性地回答了谱稀疏化后邻接谱半径的失真问题，为NIMFA流行病阈值和谱聚类等应用提供了理论保障。

Abstract: Spielman-Srivastava spectral sparsification preserves Laplacian quadratic forms to within (1 +/- epsilon), but does not directly control the adjacency spectral radius lambda_1, which governs the NIMFA epidemic threshold and arises in spectral clustering. We prove |lambda_1(A_H) - lambda_1(A_G)| <= epsilon(2 Delta - lambda_1) deterministically, with a sharp epsilon*lambda_1 bound for reweighting sparsifiers via Perron-Frobenius monotonicity. Under effective-resistance sampling, Matrix Bernstein gives O(epsilon Delta / sqrt(c)) with high probability. Combining eigenvector delocalization with resolvent perturbation theory, we establish that for graphs with delocalized Perron eigenvectors and spectral gap = Omega(Delta), the distortion is O(epsilon Delta sqrt(log n) / sqrt(n)) + O(epsilon^2 Delta^2 / delta_gap), with corollaries for Erdos-Renyi graphs, regular expanders, and stochastic block models. Lower bounds establish tightness for regular graphs.

</details>

### [166] [Amortized Neural Optimization for Pre-Layout Signal Integrity Design Space Exploration using Differentiable Surrogates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07463)
*Julian Withöft,Werner John,Emre Ecik,Ralf Brüning,Jürgen Götze*

Main category: eess.SP

TL;DR: 本文提出摊销神经优化（ANO）方法，用完全可微的神经网络替代传统迭代式黑盒优化，将高速信号完整性设计中的优化过程离线训练为全局策略，推理时仅需一次前向传播即可得到近似最优设计参数，在牺牲约10%最优性的前提下实现三到四个数量级的加速。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统预布局信号完整性设计空间探索受限于迭代式黑盒优化的计算成本，多角点扫描开销巨大，亟需一种能消除迭代推理的高效优化方法。

Method: 利用完全可微的神经网络代理模型提取解析梯度，离线训练全局优化策略（摊销优化），推理时直接将通道上下文映射到接近最优的设计参数，仅需一次确定性前向传播。

Result: 在DDR5 DFE、9维SerDes Tx/Rx联合均衡、DDR3 DQS差分对布线等场景中，相比实例级黑盒算法牺牲约10%最优性，但实现三到四个数量级加速；32万实例多角点SerDes扫描从数天缩短至毫秒级。

Abstract: Pre-layout design space exploration (DSE) for high-speed signal integrity (SI) analysis is often limited by the computational cost of simulations and iterative optimization algorithms within modern electronic design automation (EDA) workflows. While machine learning surrogate models accelerate the simulation step, optimizing designs still requires utilizing iterative black-box search methods. This iterative nature scales poorly, making multi-corner sweeps computationally expensive. As a solution, this paper proposes amortized neural optimization (ANO) for pre-layout SI design. ANO entirely eliminates iterative black-box inference by utilizing fully differentiable neural network surrogate models. ANO extracts analytical gradients from the surrogate to train a global optimization policy. Instead of solving the optimization problem repeatedly at inference, the optimization process is learned offline and therefore amortized. Once the ANO policy is trained, it maps different channel contexts directly to near-optimal design parameters in a single deterministic forward pass. The efficiency and accuracy of the ANO framework are demonstrated based on three complex SI design scenarios, including DDR5 decision feedback equalization (DFE), 9-dimensional SerDes Tx/Rx co-equalization, and DDR3 DQS differential pair routing to optimize eye diagram metrics under intra-pair skew constraints. By trading roughly 10% in optimality compared to instance-specific black-box algorithms, it realizes speedups of three to four orders of magnitude. For a large-scale 320,000-instance multi-corner SerDes sweep optimization, ANO collapses what would have taken days of computation using iterative search algorithms into a single batched forward pass that completes in milliseconds. This transforms computationally expensive SI optimization into real-time and interactive pre-layout DSE.

### [167] [Unified Geometry-Guided ML-FTLE for Tracking Transient Chaos from Scalar Time Series](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07385)
*S. V. Manivelan,Andrei Velichko,I. Manimehan*

Main category: nlin.CD

TL;DR: 提出了一种几何引导的机器学习框架，无需控制方程即可从标量观测中检测瞬态混沌，通过融合轨迹发散预测与宏观吸引子形态来追踪突发 regime shift。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 从标量观测中检测瞬态混沌且无需控制方程是非线性动力学中的根本性挑战，现有方法难以在无模型条件下准确追踪突发 regime shift。

Method: 利用k近邻预测误差提取局部不稳定尺度（ML-FTLE估计器），将其映射到Poincaré占据网格的结构相似矩阵上，通过偏最小二乘回归提取与经验有限时间Lyapunov谱校准的潜几何成分（Poincaré几何引导FTLE）。

Result: 融合拓扑状态空间与预测发散性可系统性提升连续过渡追踪效果；SSIM最优分辨逐渐阻尼，Hausdorff距离在相空间骤变时表现极端鲁棒；宏观空间离散化作为拓扑正则化器可抵抗加性高斯噪声。

Conclusion: 该无方程框架为监测复杂非平稳系统中的结构转变提供了高精度、抗噪声的诊断工具。

Abstract: Detecting transient chaos from scalar observations without governing equations represents a fundamental challenge in nonlinear dynamics. We propose a geometry-guided machine learning framework that unifies predictive trajectory divergence with macroscopic attractor morphology to track abrupt regime shifts. The methodology extracts a local instability scale via out-of-sample k-nearest neighbor forecast errors to establish the ML-FTLE estimator, subsequently mapping this temporal divergence onto a structural closeness matrix derived from a minimal dictionary of Poincare occupancy grids. By employing partial least squares regression, we extract a latent geometric component calibrated directly to the empirical finite-time Lyapunov spectrum, yielding the Poincare-based geometric-guided FTLE. Validation against analytical QR-FTLE baselines confirms that fusing topological state spaces with predictive divergence systematically improves continuous transition tracking. The Structural Similarity Index optimally resolves gradual damping, while Hausdorff Distance exhibits extreme resilience during abrupt phase-space collapses. Furthermore, macroscopic spatial discretization acts as a robust topological regularizer against additive Gaussian noise, preserving deterministic signatures even at moderate signal thresholds. This equation-free framework provides a highly accurate, noise-resilient diagnostic for monitoring structural transitions in complex non-stationary systems.

### [168] [FLOWREADER: Min-Cost Flow Optimization for Multi-Modal Long Document Q&A](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07235)
*Ambuj Mehrish,Sebatiano Vascon*

Main category: cs.IR

TL;DR: FLOWREADER将证据组装转化为最小代价流问题，在多模态节点图上统一控制评分、路由、选择和自适应计算，在碎片化多模态证据场景下表现优于top-k检索方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 长文档多模态检索中，证据碎片化分布于文本、表格、幻灯片之间，top-k分块检索将每个片段独立处理，无法捕捉证据之间的关联关系，导致答案组装困难。

Method: 将证据组装建模为多模态节点图上的最小代价流问题，用单一评分向量h控制源选择（MMR）、汇选择（长度感知可回答性代理）及每条边的代价和容量；最优流分解为候选证据路径，通过熵正则化复制动力学选择紧凑非冗余子集，并行VLM工作器在双过程门控下生成答案，低一致性或流紧张时触发单次System-2精炼。

Result: 在VisDoMBench上，FLOWREADER在碎片化证据主导的PaperTab（58.40，+1.30）和SlideVQA（72.93，+0.62）上取得最佳，在SPIQA、FetaTab、SciGraphQA上具有竞争力；五个子集宏平均65.47，与最强基线G²-Reader（66.21）差距仅0.74。

Conclusion: 最小代价流方法在碎片化多模态证据场景下表现优异，而top-k检索在此类场景中失效；该方法提供了一个统一框架来协同控制评分、路由、选择和自适应计算。

Abstract: Long, multimodal documents force retrieval-augmented systems to assemble answers from evidence fragmented across text, tables, and slides broken across cells in a long table, spread over multiple slides, or split between a figure and its discussion. Top-$k$ chunk retrieval treats each fragment independently and cannot represent how evidence connects. We introduce FLOWREADER, which reframes evidence assembly as a min-cost flow problem on a multimodal node graph: a single scoring vector $h$ controls source selection (via MMR), sink selection (via a length-aware answerability proxy), and the costs and capacities of every edge. The optimal flow is decomposed into candidate evidence paths, a compact non-redundant subset is selected by entropy-regularized replicator dynamics, and parallel VLM workers under a dual-process gate produce the answer with a single System-2 refinement pass triggered when answer consistency is low or the routed flow is strained. On VisDoMBench, FLOWREADER is best on the two subsets dominated by fragmented evidence PaperTab ($58.40$, $+1.30$ over G^{2}-Reader) and SlideVQA ($72.93$, $+0.62$) and competitive on SPIQA, FetaTab, and SciGraphQA. Macro-averaged across all five subsets, FLOWREADER ($65.47$) is within $0.74$ of the strongest baseline (G^{2}-Reader, $66.21$). Overall, these results show that min-cost flow performs well on fragmented multimodal evidence, where top-$k$ retrieval fails. It also provides a unified way to control scoring, routing, selection, and adaptive compute together.

</details>

Naive aggregation of performance metrics (e.g., averaging NDCG over benchmarks) can yield misleading rankings, undermining practical selection. To address this problem, we introduce a novel, data-driven ranking methodology based on Bradley-Terry (BT) model. We demonstrate that the obtained ranking depends on key dataset statistics. Additionally, we propose a novel metric for evaluating ranking consistency and demonstrate robustness of our ranking to incomplete data. Finally, we introduce a dataset-specific methodology for ranking algorithms on unseen datasets without running the models, relying on extensions of the Bradley-Terry framework, including BT trees and BT models with covariates.

### [170] [Principles of Concept Representation in Sentence Encoders](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06994)
*Isabelle Mohr,John Dujany,Jonathan Souquet,Andre Freitas*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文通过表示组合性视角研究了句子编码器产生良好概念表示的条件，提出了四个原则：微调仅重新校准而非扩展潜在几何（P1）；语义信号集中在最终Transformer层（P2）；硬负样本改善判别与鲁棒性但不改善检索排序（P3）；监督有效性依赖于目标概念的组合类型，外延式训练对交叠性和下义性家族有效但损害关系性和内涵性家族（P4）。同时发布了两个新评估数据集。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究句子编码器何时以及为何能产生良好的概念表示，通过表示组合性的理论框架来预测当前编码器的成功与失败之处。

Method: 在WordNet和Wiktionary的330万同义词和定义对上，对编码器条件进行受控消融实验，在三个去污染分割和一个修饰语标注的名词短语基准上评估，识别出四个原则。

Result: 识别出四个原则（P1-P4），揭示了微调的本质、语义信号分布、硬负样本的特定作用以及监督训练与概念组合类型之间的结构性不匹配。

Conclusion: 当前训练范式存在结构性局限：外延式训练有利于交叠性和下义性概念家族，但会损害关系性和内涵性概念家族，表明需要针对不同概念类型设计差异化的监督策略。

Abstract: What makes a sentence encoder produce good concept representations? We approach this through the lens of representational compositionality: an encoder supports a concept family only when its latent space admits a low-distortion realization of the corresponding semantic operator. This framing predicts both where current encoders succeed and where they are structurally mismatched to their supervision. Through a controlled ablation over encoder conditions trained on 3.3 million synonym and definition pairs from WordNet and Wiktionary, evaluated on three decontaminated splits and a modifier-labeled noun-phrase benchmark, we identify four principles. Fine-tuning recalibrates the latent geometry rather than expanding it (P1). Semantic signal concentrates in the final transformer layer before concept-specific training begins, making cross-layer pooling redundant (P2). Hard negatives improve discrimination and stress-test robustness without improving retrieval ranking, showing that calibration and ranking are independently addressable (P3). Finally, the effectiveness of supervision depends on the composition type of the target concept. Extensional training helps intersective and subsective families while degrading relational and intensional ones, exposing a structural limitation of current training paradigms (P4). We release two new evaluation datasets: a DBpedia semantic-gap benchmark and a modifier-labeled NP paraphrase suite.

</details>


### [171] [TRACE: Trajectory Reasoning through Adaptive Cross-Step Evidence Aggregation for LLM Agents](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07054)
*Vijitha Mittapalli,Shreyaa Jayant Dani,Satya Srujana Pilli,Snigdha Ansu,Mohammadreza Teymoorianfard,Franck Dernoncourt,Hongjie Chen,Yu Wang,Ryan A. Rossi,Nesreen K. Ahmed*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: TRACE是一个针对长程LLM智能体轨迹的监控框架，通过TIJ（分流-检查-判断）循环来检测隐藏的恶意目标，在SHADE-Arena的十个任务域上达到了0.713的F1分数和0.844的召回率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法要么一次性评估整个轨迹，要么将轨迹分割成独立窗口独立评分，无法连接时间上分散的证据，难以检测通过一系列看似良性行为实现隐藏恶意目标的LLM智能体。

Method: 提出TRACE框架，采用TIJ（Triage-Inspect-Judge）循环：识别高信号区域、进行定向检查并在推理步骤间累积证据、综合生成轨迹级别的判定。

Result: 在SHADE-Arena的十个任务域上，TRACE的聚合F1得分为0.713，召回率为0.844，在需要远距离证据链接的任务上提升最大。

Conclusion: TRACE通过累进证据积累和长程链接能力，有效提升了长程LLM智能体轨迹中恶意行为的检测性能。

Abstract: Autonomous LLM agents can pursue hidden malicious objectives through sequences of individually benign actions, making sabotage difficult to detect using standard trajectory-level monitoring. Existing approaches either evaluate complete trajectories in a single pass or partition them into independently scored windows, limiting their ability to connect evidence across temporally distant actions. We propose TRACE, a monitoring framework for long-horizon LLM agent trajectories. TRACE operates through a TIJ (Triage-Inspect-Judge) loop that identifies high-signal regions, performs targeted inspection while maintaining accumulated evidence across reasoning steps, and synthesizes a trajectory-level verdict. We evaluate TRACE on ten task domains from SHADE-Arena against state-of-the-art baselines. TRACE achieves an aggregate F1 of 0.713 and recall of 0.844, with the largest gains on tasks requiring long-range evidence linking.

</details>


### [172] [SigmaScale: LLM Compression with SVD-based Low-Rank Decomposition and Learned Scaling Matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07098)
*Ernests Lavrinovics,Marco Letizia,Roy Janco,Shai Segal,Johannes Bjerva,Maurizio Pierini*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: SigmaScale提出通过学习辅助缩放矩阵来改进基于截断SVD的大语言模型压缩方法，通过激活感知的压缩损失优化行/列缩放变换，在Llama 3.1 8B和Qwen3-8B上取得有竞争力的结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有SVD压缩方法中缩放矩阵多通过解析方式推导，缺乏灵活性；本文旨在通过学习方式获得更适应模型权重结构的激活感知缩放变换，以提升压缩效果。

Method: 学习两组向量定义对角行/列缩放变换矩阵S，在激活感知的压缩损失下进行优化；利用学习到的缩放降低权重矩阵的有效本征秩（通过有效本征熵衡量），实现更灵活的低秩压缩。

Result: 在Llama 3.1 8B Instruct和Qwen3-8B上，SigmaScale在困惑度和零样本基准测试中与最先进的SVD压缩方法竞争力相当；学习到的缩放有效降低了有效本征秩，且该降低与压缩损失强相关。

Conclusion: SigmaScale提供了一种更灵活的低秩LLM压缩途径，能适应单个权重的结构，在特定任务上展现优势，是降低LLM推理计算成本的有效选项。

Abstract: We present SigmaScale, a method for learning auxiliary scaling matrices $S$ to aid truncated Singular Value Decomposition (SVD) based Large Language Model (LLM) compression. Instead of deriving scaling matrices analytically, SigmaScale optimizes two sets of vectors that define diagonal row and column scaling transformations under an activation-aware compression loss. We show that learned scaling lowers the effective intrinsic rank of weight matrices, as reflected by reductions in effective-rank entropy, and that this reduction is strongly correlated with compression loss. Experiments on Llama 3.1 8B Instruct and Qwen3-8B show that SigmaScale is competitive with closely related state-of-the-art SVD-based compression methods across perplexity and zero-shot benchmarks. By using learned activation-aware transformations, SigmaScale explores a more flexible route to low-rank LLM compression by adapting to the structure of individual model weights. The advantage observed in specific tasks makes our approach a valid option for applications requiring a reduced LLM-inference computing cost.

</details>


### [173] [When Large Language Models Fail in Healthcare: Evaluating Sensitivity to Prompt Variations](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07237)
*Mahdi Alkaeed*

Main category: cs.CL

TL;DR: 本文系统评估了通用型（GPT-3.5, Llama3）和医学专用型LLM（ClinicalBERT, BioLlama3, BioBERT）对提示扰动的鲁棒性，发现即使是微小措辞变化也可能改变临床建议，对抗性扰动可引发危险输出，表明这些模型在医疗高风险场景中不可靠。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LLM在医疗领域（临床问答、诊断支持、报告总结）应用日益广泛，但模型对词汇和句法层面的提示扰动高度敏感，在安全关键的临床场景中可能造成严重后果，因此有必要系统评估其鲁棒性。

Method: 使用MedMCQA基准，将扰动分为自然扰动和对抗性扰动两类，对通用型LLM（GPT-3.5, Llama3）和医学专用LLM（ClinicalBERT, BioLlama3, BioBERT）进行系统性敏感性分析，评估模型在临床推理任务中的一致性、准确性和可靠性。

Result: 1. 医学LLM并非固有安全，微小的措辞变化即可改变临床建议；2. 模型对简单的词汇替换或释义具有韧性，但常在句法重排或误导性上下文线索下崩溃；3. 对抗性扰动可产生危险输出，如推荐错误剂量或遗漏关键发现；4. 该脆弱性在通用型与领域专用模型中均普遍存在。

Conclusion: 在高风险的医疗场景中，LLM因改写输入而改变诊断或产生幻觉药物是不可接受的，这类模型尚不能被临床医生可靠信任。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in healthcare for tasks such as clinical question answering, diagnosis support, and report summarization. Despite their promise, these models remain highly sensitive to subtle prompt perturbations, both lexical and syntactic, posing serious risks in safety-critical clinical applications. In this study, we conduct a systematic sensitivity analysis to evaluate the robustness of both general-purpose (e.g., GPT-3.5, Llama3) and medical-specific LLMs (e.g., ClinicalBERT, BioLlama3, BioBERT) using the MedMCQA benchmark. We categorize perturbations into natural and adversarial types and examine their effect on model consistency, accuracy, and reliability in clinical reasoning tasks. Our findings reveal that medical LLMs are not intrinsically safe. Even minor variations in phrasing can alter clinical advice, and targeted adversarial prompts can provoke harmful outputs. In high-stakes settings like healthcare, such unpredictability is unacceptable-models that change diagnoses due to reworded inputs or hallucinate medications when slightly rephrased cannot be reliably trusted by clinicians. While models tend to show resilience to simple lexical substitutions or paraphrasing, they often break down under syntactic reordering or misleading contextual cues. This fragility is evident across both general-purpose and domain-specific LLMs. Notably, adversarial manipulations can lead to clinically dangerous outputs, such as recommending incorrect dosages or omitting critical findings.

### [174] [The Proxy Benders Decomposition](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07403)
*Changkun Guan,El Mehdi Er Raqabi,Mathieu Tanneau,Pascal Van Hentenryck*

Main category: math.OC

TL;DR: 本文提出代理Benders分解（Proxy-BD）框架，通过自监督预测-投影-补全机制生成可行的代理解来替代子问题的精确求解，在保持理论有效性的同时大幅提升计算效率，在2000x2000规模的设施选址问题上实现最高161倍加速和240倍以上的割数量减少。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 经典Benders分解在每次迭代中重复求解高度相似的子问题，且容易出现zigzagging行为，导致大规模场景下收敛缓慢。研究者希望通过利用子问题的重复性和参数化结构，用代理模型替代精确求解来加速。

Method: 提出Proxy-BD框架，核心是自监督的预测-投影-补全（predict-project-and-complete）机制：首先预测子问题解，然后通过投影和补全层确保生成对偶可行解，从而保证产生的Benders割在理论上始终有效。该框架可自然扩展到分支-Benders割算法等现代分解方案。

Result: 在2000x2000规模的设施选址和网络设计问题上，Proxy-BD达到中位最优性差距低于0.5%，最高实现161倍中位加速，割的数量减少超过240倍。计算增益随问题复杂度的增加而增大。

Conclusion: 代理推断在大规模分解场景中比重复精确子问题优化具有显著更好的可扩展性，为大规模混合整数优化提供了一种高效且理论上可靠的替代方案。

Abstract: Benders decomposition is a fundamental framework for solving large-scale mixed-integer optimization problems with complicating variables that, when fixed, yield significantly easier subproblems. However, classical Benders decomposition repeatedly solves highly similar subproblems and often exhibits zigzagging behavior across iterations, leading to slow convergence in large-scale settings. Motivated by the repetitive structure and parametric nature of Benders subproblems, this paper introduces the proxy Benders decomposition (Proxy-BD), a new decomposition framework in which subproblem optimization is replaced by certified optimization proxies rather than repeated exact solves.
  The proposed proxy follows a self-supervised predict-project-and-complete mechanism that produces dual-feasible solutions for generating provably valid Benders cuts. The framework preserves the theoretical validity of the decomposition independently of prediction quality through a projection-and-completion certification layer. A formal characterization of proxy-induced cuts is established, and the framework naturally extends to modern decomposition schemes, including branch-and-Benders-cut algorithms.
  Computational experiments on large-scale facility location and network design problems demonstrate that Proxy-BD substantially reduces the computational effort of subproblems while maintaining near-optimal solution quality. On large-scale uncapacitated facility location instances up to 2000x2000, Proxy-BD achieves median optimality gaps below 0.5%, yields up to 161x median speedups, and reduces the number of generated cuts by more than 240x on the largest instances. The computational gains consistently increase with recourse complexity, indicating that proxy-based inference scales substantially more favorably than repeated exact subproblem optimization in large-scale decomposition settings.

</details>

### [175] [Lean4Agent: Formal Modeling and Verification for Agent Workflow and Trajectory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06523)
*Ruida Wang,Jerry Huang,Pengcheng Wang,Xuanqing Liu,Luyang Kong,Tong Zhang*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出Lean4Agent框架，利用依赖类型形式语言Lean4对LLM工作流进行形式化建模、验证与调试，实验表明通过验证的工作流性能平均提升11.94%，且LeanEvolve可进一步改进工作流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前LLM智能体系统缺乏形式化方法来指定、验证和调试工作流与执行轨迹，这类似于自然语言歧义性问题，因而受形式语言启发，引入Lean4来建模和验证智能体行为。

Method: 提出Lean4Agent框架，包含FormalAgentLib（可扩展的Lean4库，用于形式化建模与验证工作流语义一致性）和LeanEvolve（利用验证结果修正工作流以提升能力）。

Result: 在SWE-Bench-Verified和ELAIP-Bench子集上，验证通过的工作流比未通过的平均高11.94%；LeanEvolve平均提升SWE性能7.47%。

Conclusion: Lean4Agent为使用依赖类型形式语言形式化建模和验证智能体行为建立了基础，开辟了一个新研究领域。

Abstract: Equipping Large Language Models (LLMs) to execute reliable multi-step workflows has become a central challenge in artificial intelligence. Despite recent advances in LLMs' agentic capabilities, most agent systems still lack formal methods for specifying, verifying, and debugging their workflow and execution trajectories. This challenge mirrors a long-standing problem in mathematics, where the ambiguity of natural languages (NLs) motivates the development of formal languages (FLs). Inspired by this paradigm, we propose **Lean4Agent**, to the best of our knowledge, the first framework that uses Lean4, a dependent-type FL to model and verify agent behavior. **Lean4Agent** launches **FormalAgentLib**, an extensible Lean4 library for formally modeling and verifying agent workflows' semantic consistency under explicit assumptions, and enabling localization of execution-time failures revealed by trajectories. Building on **FormalAgentLib**, we further develop **LeanEvolve**, which applies results in **FormalAgentLib** to revise workflows to enhance its capability. Extensive experiments on a hard problem subset of SWE-Bench-Verified and a subset of ELAIP-Bench across 5 leading LLMs indicate that the verification-passing workflows outperform the failing ones by an average of **11.94%**, and **LeanEvolve** further improves SWE performance by **7.47%** on average. Furthermore, **Lean4Agent** establishes a foundation for a new field of using expressive dependent-type FL to formally model and verify agent behavior.

</details>


### [176] [Declarative Skills for AI Agents in Knowledge-Grounded Tool-Use Workflows](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06923)
*M. Danish Lim,I. Danial Bin Sharudin,Wen Han Chen,Cedric Lim,Laura Wynter*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究工具使用型AI代理在客服工作流中的编排机制，比较了声明式代理（通过自然语言技能文件控制流程）、命令式代理（基于程序化状态机）和无脚手架基线代理的性能。结果表明：检索质量是主要瓶颈；在高质量检索下，声明式技能可提升程序性任务准确率并减少编排错误。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在非结构化知识库的客服工作流中，哪种编排机制（声明式vs命令式vs无脚手架）对工具使用型AI代理更有效。

Method: 将三种代理形式化为去中心化部分可观测马尔可夫决策过程（Dec-POMDP）中的策略类，分析信息论和结构特性，并在5个语言模型和2种检索机制下进行实证对比。

Result: 检索质量是所有代理的瓶颈；在高质量检索下，声明式代理在程序性任务上持续提升准确率并减少编排错误，而命令式状态机的脆弱性未能可靠提升任务成功或合规性。

Conclusion: 声明式代理是有效的编排范式，但检索质量是决定AI代理性能的关键因素，技能文件无法弥补低质量检索带来的性能损失。

Abstract: We study orchestration mechanisms for tool-using AI agents in realistic customer-service workflows over an unstructured knowledge base. We argue that declarative agents -- AI agents equipped with natural-language skill files appended to the system prompt -- are an effective orchestration paradigm. Concretely, we compare (i) a DeclarativeAgent that reads three domain-specific skill files at inference time and decides its own control flow, (ii) an ImperativeAgent based on a programmatic state machine with explicit phases, and (iii) an unscaffolded baseline agent modeled after the $τ$-Knowledge benchmark agent. Our ImperativeAgent is motivated by externalised-control inference as in Recursive Language Models and graph-based orchestration frameworks. We formalise the three agents as policy classes within a decentralised partially-observable Markov decision process and analyse their information-theoretic and structural properties; we then test the predicted differences empirically on five language models and two retrieval regimes. Our results show that retrieval quality is a dominant bottleneck for AI agents: when evidence is incomplete or skewed, all agents degrade substantially, and skill files cannot recover lost performance. Under high-quality retrieval, however, declarative skills consistently improve accuracy on procedural tasks and reduce orchestration errors, while the imperative state machine's brittleness does not reliably improve task success or compliance.

</details>


### [177] [Detecting and Mitigating Bias by Treating Fairness as a Symmetry Operation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06514)
*Nishit Singh*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出将机器学习系统中的偏见形式化为对称性破缺操作，并通过基于损失的对称性恢复正则化机制实现公平分类器，在四个合成数据集上实现了90%以上的偏见违规减少，仅以约5%的准确率成本为代价。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决机器学习系统在高风险社会经济环境中部署时普遍存在的偏见问题，现有方法通常需要因果图知识或计算负担较重。

Method: 将偏见形式化为对称性破缺操作，要求分类器在交换敏感属性（保持实质特征不变）的反事实操作下输出不变；通过基于损失的正则化作为对称性恢复机制来实现公平性。

Result: 在四个合成数据集上，该方法实现了超过90%的偏见违规减少，准确率成本仅约5%。

Conclusion: 该框架无需因果图知识、计算轻量、可泛化到任何可定义为比特翻转的敏感属性，适用于主流基准测试中缺乏的局部歧视来源场景。

Abstract: Machine learning systems deployed in high stakes socioeconomic settings routinely display bias. We formalize bias as a symmetry breaking operation: a classifier is fair if its outputs remain invariant under the counterfactual operation of switching a sensitive attribute, with merit features held fixed. We implement loss based regularization as a symmetry restoring mechanism and evaluate the framework on four synthetic datasets with varying levels of noise, correlation, and bias. The framework achieves upwards of 90\% violation reduction, with accuracy costs around 5\%. This framework does not require causal graph knowledge, is computationally lightweight, and generalizes to any sensitive attribute definable as a bit-flip, making it suitable for contexts where local sources of discrimination remain absent from mainstream benchmarks.

</details>


### [178] [DiBS: Diffusion-Informed Branch Selection](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06518)
*Bo Liu,Yuan Xie,Yuan Gao,Xiaolong Luo,Peng Ye,Tao Chen,Fujun Han*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种名为DiBS的扩散模型引导分支选择方法，用于解决数独问题。该方法保持符号求解器的完备性，利用扩散模型进行分支排序指导，在Royle 17-clue数独基准上显著降低了搜索成本，尤其在节点数、回溯次数和长尾百分位数方面表现出色。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数独求解方法存在互补性缺陷：基于学习的求解器缺乏硬正确性保证，而完整的符号求解器容易陷入长尾搜索。作者旨在结合两者的优势，提出一种既有正确性保证又能减少搜索成本的方法。

Method: DiBS方法保持符号求解器的完备性，使用扩散模型作为分支排序指导。核心方法是对当前部分赋值下的候选值进行排序，并结合轻量级一致性信号。同时提供了理论证明来解释其工作原理。

Result: 在Royle 17-clue数独基准实验上，DiBS相比强启发式基线显著降低了搜索成本，尤其在节点数、回溯次数和长尾百分位数方面。结果表明，在分支顺序错误代价最高的困难实例上，学习到的全局指导是有效的。

Conclusion: DiBS成功地将扩散模型与完整符号求解器结合，既保证了正确性，又通过全局学习指导有效减少了搜索成本，特别是在困难实例上表现优异。

Abstract: Sudoku is a representative constraint satisfaction problem that requires global structural reasoning under strict discrete constraints. The existing works of solving Sudoku mainly focus on two dominant approaches, i.e., traditional heuristic and deep learning solver. However, they suffer from two complementary limitations: learning-based solvers lack hard correctness guarantees, while complete symbolic solvers are still prone to long-tail search. To address these shortcomings, we propose a novel diffusion model-guided approach, termed as DiBS, for the branch selection search process. Specifically, DiBS keeps the symbolic solver complete and uses the diffusion model as a branch-ordering guide. The core method is ranking candidate values under the current partial assignment and lightweight consistency signal. Furthermore, we provide an in-depth theoretical proof to reveal how it works and why it works. Experiments on the challenging Royle 17-clue Sudoku benchmark show that our DiBS substantially reduces search cost relative to strong heuristic baselines, especially in nodes, backtracks, and long-tail percentiles. Besides, these results confirm that learned global guidance is effective on hard instances where branch-order mistakes are most expensive. All codes are available at https://github.com/shanxierdan/DiBS.

</details>


### [179] [SafeGene: Reusable Adapters for Transferable Safety Alignment](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06519)
*Yanghan Wang,Zhiqiang Kou,Fu Feng,Jing Wang,Xin Geng*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: SafeGene提出了一种可重用的安全适配器模块，通过将安全能力与任务特定更新解耦，跨任务复用安全表征，在保持下游性能的同时降低有害响应率。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开源大模型在下游微调过程中会削弱安全对齐，且每次更新任务数据时安全恢复问题反复出现，现有方法将安全恢复视为模型特定的修复步骤，缺乏跨任务可重用性。

Method: 1) 从对齐与退化模型的差异中提取安全表征；2) 通过数据感知的层选择精炼出可跨任务迁移的安全向量；3) 采用少样本的逐层系数重校准，将安全适配器注入下游任务模型。

Result: 在多个模型家族、下游任务和安全评估器上，SafeGene增强的模型在保持下游性能的同时降低了有害响应率，在安全-效用权衡上优于现有安全适应方法。

Conclusion: 安全能力可以作为独立、可重用的适配器表征与任务更新解耦，SafeGene提供了一种高效、通用的跨任务安全恢复方案。

Abstract: Open-weight LLMs are increasingly fine-tuned into customized assistants, but downstream fine-tuning can weaken safety alignment and make models more vulnerable to malicious prompts, even when the training data is not intentionally harmful. This creates a recurring safety recovery problem as target models are repeatedly updated with new task data or user interactions. We propose SafeGene, a reusable safety-adapter module designed for cross-task reuse within each architecture-compatible model family. Rather than treating safety recovery as a model-specific repair step, SafeGene treats safety capability as an independent, reusable adapter representation decoupled from task-specific updates. This representation is obtained from aligned--degraded model discrepancies, refined into task-transferable safety vectors through data-aware layer selection, and expressed in each downstream task-adapted model via few-shot layer-wise coefficient recalibration. Experiments across multiple model families, downstream tasks, and safety judges show that SafeGene-enhanced models reduce harmful response rates while maintaining downstream performance, outperforming representative safe adaptation methods in safety--utility trade-off.

</details>


### [180] [CrowdMath: A Dataset of Crowdsourced Mathematical Research Discussions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06526)
*Sherin Muckatira,Jesse Geneson,Slava Gerovitch,Pavel Etingof,Mikhail Gronas,Anna Rumshisky*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文介绍CrowdMath数据集，包含164条来自MIT PRIMES-AoPS CrowdMath项目（2016-2025）的专家标注的协作数学问题求解链，用于评估大语言模型在协作式开放问题求解中的能力。实验表明，前沿模型在下一帖预测任务上表现尚可（83-88%准确率），但在理解单个帖子的功能角色（如部分进展、错误识别等）方面表现较差（macro-F1仅0.42），揭示了模型在理解协作数学进展方面存在显著差距。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有数学推理基准主要评估格式良好的问题求解（有最终答案、逐步解答或完整证明），未能捕捉协作式开放问题求解过程——参与者提出部分论点、识别错误、修复有缺陷的推理，并逐步将零散贡献综合成完整证明。作者旨在填补这一评估空白。

Method: 构建CrowdMath数据集：从MIT PRIMES-AoPS CrowdMath项目（2016-2025）中收集164条专家标注的进展链，每条链追踪从开放问题陈述到完成证明的多参与者论坛讨论过程。帖子按其在求解过程中的功能角色（部分进展、证明完成、错误推理、错误识别等）进行标注。定义评估任务，对6个前沿模型进行基准测试。

Result: 模型在下一帖预测任务上达到83-88%的准确率，表明能跟踪局部讨论流。但在帖子角色分类任务上，最佳模型仅取得0.42的macro-F1分数，表现不佳。

Conclusion: CrowdMath数据集暴露了当前大语言模型在解决格式良好的数学问题与理解协作式数学进展之间的差距，为评估和改进模型在真实协作数学推理场景中的能力提供了重要基准。

Abstract: Large language models have made substantial progress on mathematical reasoning, but existing benchmarks typically evaluate well-specified problems with final answers, step-by-step solutions, or complete proofs. They do not capture collaborative open-problem solving: a setting in which participants propose partial arguments, identify gaps or errors in prior steps, repair flawed reasoning, and gradually synthesize incremental contributions into a proof. We introduce CrowdMath, a dataset of 164 expert-annotated progress chains from the MIT PRIMES--Art of Problem Solving (AoPS) CrowdMath program (2016-2025), a collaborative research initiative whose discussions have led to peer-reviewed publications. Each chain traces a multi-participant forum discussion from an open-problem statement to a completed proof. Posts are labeled by their functional roles in the evolving solution process, including partial progress, proof completion, erroneous reasoning, and error identification. We define evaluation tasks and benchmark six frontier models. Models achieve 83-88% accuracy on next-post prediction, suggesting that they can follow the local flow of mathematical discussion. However, they struggle to identify the functional significance of individual contributions with the best model achieving only 0.42 macro-F1 on post-role classification. CrowdMath exposes a gap between solving well-specified mathematical problems and understanding collaborative mathematical progress as it unfolds.

</details>


### [181] [Attack Selection in Agentic AI Control Evaluations Meaningfully Decreases Safety](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06529)
*Catherine Ge-Wang,Tyler Crosse,Benjamin Hadad,Joachim Schaeffer,Ram Potham,Tyler Tracy*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文研究了AI控制评估中攻击者的策略性攻击选择能力，发现通过启动策略和停止策略可以显著降低系统的实证安全性，表明现有评估方法可能高估了对抗选择性攻击者的安全性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有AI控制评估通常假设攻击者不会策略性地选择攻击时机，但这种假设不现实，因为策略性攻击者更难被发现。作者旨在研究攻击选择能力对AI控制协议安全性的影响。

Method: 将攻击决策分解为两个策略：启动策略（决定何时开始攻击）和停止策略（决定何时中止进行中的攻击）。在BashArena和LinuxArena两个智能体环境中进行实验，在1%审计预算下测试两种策略的效果。

Result: 在1%审计预算下，启动策略在BashArena和LinuxArena上均降低安全性20个百分点；停止策略在BashArena上降低20个百分点，在LinuxArena上降低28个百分点。这些降低被视为攻击选择效应的上界。

Conclusion: 现有控制评估可能对策略性攻击者给出过于乐观的安全估计。建议未来的评估、系统卡片和安全案例应诱导攻击选择行为，以产生更现实的安全估计。

Abstract: An attacker that strategically chooses when to attack is much harder to catch than one that attacks indiscriminately. AI control is a safety framework for deploying capable but untrusted AI agents under the oversight of a weaker, trusted monitor and a limited human audit budget. Control evaluations stress-test these protocols by pitting a red-team attack policy against the blue-team monitor, but current evaluations typically assume attackers that do not strategically select when to attack. We study this capability, attack selection, in agentic settings by decomposing attack decisions into a start policy, which decides when an attacker should attack, and a stop policy, which decides when an attacker should abort an ongoing attack. Across two agentic settings, BashArena and LinuxArena, both policies substantially lower measured empirical safety without changing the underlying attack capability. At a 1% audit budget, our start policy reduces safety by 20pp on both BashArena and LinuxArena, and our stop policy reduces safety by 20pp on BashArena and 28pp on LinuxArena. These reductions should be interpreted as upper bounds on the effect of attack selection. Existing control evaluations may therefore yield overly optimistic safety estimates against selective attackers. We recommend that future evaluations, system cards, and safety cases elicit attack selection to produce more realistic safety estimates.

</details>


### [182] [Online Pandora's Box for Contextual LLM Cascading](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07392)
*Alexandre Belloni,Yan Chen,Yehua Wei*

Main category: cs.AI

TL;DR: 本文针对LLM级联场景，提出了一种在线上下文Pandora's Box模型，用于自适应地查询和选择LLM API。通过直接建模保留索引而非完整分布，结合GMM估计和UCB置信界，实现了维度相关的$\widetilde O(\sqrt T)$累积遗憾。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在大语言模型级联场景中，决策者需要自适应地查询多个LLM API并选择最佳输出，但传统Pandora's Box模型的反馈结构（直接揭示奖励）不适用于此——查询API仅揭示输出而非奖励，奖励只在最终部署后获得。现有方法需要估计每个API的完整条件输出和成本分布，复杂且样本效率低。

Method: 提出在线上下文Pandora's Box模型，包含两阶段决策：查询阶段顺序查询API并产生输出依赖成本，选择阶段部署一个输出并观察下游奖励。不估计完整分布，而是直接建模基于Weitzman策略的上下文保留索引函数（参数化结构），采用GMM型估计结合UCB置信界，同时为保留索引和共享的输出级奖励评估器构建置信上界。

Result: 在正则性条件下，所提策略在T个周期内实现了维度相关的$\widetilde O(\sqrt T)$累积遗憾。

Conclusion: 本文成功将经典Pandora's Box模型扩展到具有输出中介反馈的在线上下文场景，通过保留索引的参数量化消除了对完整分布估计的依赖，为LLM API级联选择提供了理论基础和可行的学习算法。

Abstract: Motivated by Large Language Model (LLM) cascading, we propose an online contextual Pandora's Box model for adaptively querying and selecting LLM APIs. In each period, a decision-maker observes a request context and faces a two-phase decision problem. In the query phase, the decision-maker sequentially queries APIs, where each query reveals a generated output and the decision-maker incurs an (output-dependent) cost. In the selection phase, the decision-maker selects one of the generated outputs to deploy and observes only the downstream reward of the deployed output. This output-mediated feedback structure differs from classical online contextual Pandora's Box models, in which opening a box directly reveals its reward.
  Rather than estimating the full conditional output and cost distributions of each API, we directly model the reservation index and develop a learning approach for the query phase. Specifically, we impose a parametric structure on the contextual reservation index functions induced by the classical Weitzman's policy. Our policy combines generalized method of moments (GMM) type estimation of these reservation indices with UCB-style confidence bounds for both these indices and the shared output-level reward evaluator. Under regularity conditions, we prove that the resulting policy achieves dimension-dependent $\widetilde O(\sqrt T)$ cumulative regret over a horizon of $T$ periods.

</details>

### [183] [Probabilistic learning to perform pre-onset individualised prediction of disease severity: application to Veno Occlusive Disease](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06516)
*Dalia Chakrabarty,Kane Warrior,Chuqiao Zhang,Akash Bhojgaria,Joydeep Chakrabartty*

Main category: q-bio.QM

TL;DR: 提出一种基于随机过程的概率监督学习方法，利用回顾性患者数据和概率逆学习构建增强训练集，实现对骨髓移植后肝静脉闭塞病（VOD）严重程度的早期个性化预测，辅助临床治疗决策。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有方法无法在移植前可靠地、自动化地、早期地个性化预测疾病严重程度，导致医生难以提前制定最优治疗方案（如是否使用Defibrotide）。

Method: 1. 将疾病变量与严重程度评分之间的关系建模为高斯随机过程的一个样本函数；
2. 利用回顾性患者队列的真实演化数据生成初始训练集；
3. 通过概率逆学习（从未来患者数据反推评分）扩充训练集；
4. 基于扩充后的训练集学习预测函数，实现移植前自动化评分预测。

Result: 能够对VOD严重程度评分进行早期个性化预测，并已开发出AI工具供医生输入数据、获取预测结果。

Conclusion: 该方法为移植前VOD严重性预测提供了可靠、自动化的AI解决方案，可辅助血液肿瘤科医生制定个性化治疗方案（如是否使用Defibrotide），具有临床转化潜力。

Abstract: We advance a new probabilistic supervised learning approach that permits reliable, automated, and early individualised prediction of the severity with which a disease will develop in a prospective patient. The prediction capacity is illustrated via the pre-transplant prediction of the score of severity of Veno Occlusive Disease (or VOD) in the digital twin (DT) of the considered prospective patient, where this score parametrises the severity with which VOD will develop in this patient, after they undergo their Bone Marrow Transplant. The learning of the relationship between the pre-transplant variables, and a severity score variable is undertaken by modelling this relationship as a (random) function that is treated as a sample function of an adequately-chosen stochastic process. The parameters of this underlying process are learnt using a training dataset that is generated using the real-time evolution of retrospective patients in a cohort, with this training dataset subsequently augmented in size by a probabilistic inverse learning of the score of prospective patients. The augmented training set, then permits the learning of the function that capacitates - at the pre-transplant stage - automated prediction of the score of the severity of VOD that characterises the DT of a physical patient in their unique pre-transplant state. This score is subsequently fed back to the real prospective patient as the severity with which VOD will develop in them, after this patient undergoes their transplant. Such a score then permits the treating Haematologist-Oncologists to decide on the treatment regimen, which in this illustration reduces to deciding on treating the patient with Defibrotide. An AI facility is developed to undertake such automated prediction, with the physician inputting the data on the pre-transplant state that characterises the DT of the prospective patient under consideration.

</details>

### [184] [Multiscale POD of Transformer Attention Fields: Scale-Selective Analysis via Morlet Scalogram](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06573)
*Athanasios Zeris*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文提出尺度选择POD方法，利用连续小波变换和POD从Transformer注意力场中提取不同尺度的能量主导模态，揭示了注意力场的层次化尺度组织特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有工作缺乏对Transformer注意力场中多尺度结构的系统性分析，受湍流分析中POD方法的启发，作者希望建立一种无监督、无需修改架构的注意力场模态分析框架。

Method: 利用Morlet连续小波变换识别注意力滞后结构中的主导时间尺度，再对各尺度上的注意力场进行POD分解，提取能量主导模态；定义谱集中指数（基于POD特征值衰减率）量化各层的注意力场复杂度。

Result: 发现早期注意力层倾向于细尺度模态，后期层转向粗尺度；谱集中指数能够有效区分不同层的注意力场复杂度；POD模态满足L2重建误差最优性定理，提供数据驱动的有效秩。

Conclusion: 该方法无需修改架构或依赖语言标注，仅从集成统计量中即可提取主导注意力模式，为理解Transformer内部表征的尺度结构提供了新视角。

Abstract: We introduce scale-selective Proper Orthogonal Decomposition (POD) for transformer attention fields, inspired by the use of POD for extracting energetically dominant modes from turbulent flow ensembles. The Morlet continuous wavelet transform identifies dominant temporal scales in the attention lag structure across a document ensemble; POD then extracts the energetically dominant modes at each scale from the ensemble of attention fields. The resulting modes reveal layer-dependent scale organisation, with early layers emphasising fine scales and later layers shifting toward coarser scales. We define a spectral concentration index from the POD eigenvalue decay rate and show empirically that it differentiates layers by their attention field complexity. By the classical POD optimality theorem, the extracted modes minimise the average L2 reconstruction error over the ensemble (Theorem 1), giving a data-driven effective rank for each layer. The method requires no architectural modification and no linguistic annotations: dominant attention patterns emerge from ensemble statistics alone. The turbulence analogy is structural rather than physical: we borrow ensemble covariance and modal analysis, not fluid dynamics itself.

### [185] [Depth over Fidelity in Fixed-Budget Noisy Evolution Strategies](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06555)
*Sichen Wang,Zhipeng Lu*

Main category: cs.NE

TL;DR: 本文提出概率精英成员（PEM）方法，通过条件期望秩权重替代硬排名权重，解决进化策略在固定评估预算下的深度-保真度权衡问题。残差自举PEM（RB-PEM）在COCO bbob-noisy及RL策略搜索等任务中，于高错排、预算受限场景下取得一致改进。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在固定评估预算下，噪声进化策略面临深度-保真度权衡：增加组内去噪评估会减少可执行的分布更新次数。作者主张深度优先（更多分布更新）而非保真度，并寻求在保留条件均值更新的同时减少更新方差的方法。

Method: 提出概率精英成员（PEM），用条件期望秩权重替代硬排名权重，这是一种对噪声秩步的Rao-Blackwell化。通过残差自举（RB-PEM）实现，每代额外开销有上限；并辅以自适应探针-切换机制应对低噪声场景。

Result: 在COCO bbob-noisy套件、RL策略搜索和超参数优化等外部任务中，RB-PEM在高错排、预算受限场景下始终优于基线方法。

Conclusion: 在固定评估预算下，进化策略应优先深度（更多分布更新）而非保真度（组内去噪）；PEM方法通过Rao-Blackwell化有效降低了噪声排名步的更新离散度。

Abstract: Noisy evolution strategies under fixed evaluation budgets face a depth-fidelity trade-off: spending evaluations to denoise intra-generation rankings reduces the number of distribution updates the optimizer can execute. We argue for depth over fidelity and propose probabilistic elite membership (PEM), which replaces hard rank-based weights in evolution strategies with conditional expected rank weights that integrate over ranking uncertainty. PEM preserves the conditional mean update while reducing conditional update dispersion, a Rao-Blackwellization of the noisy rank-based step. We instantiate PEM via residual bootstrapping (RB-PEM) with capped per-generation overhead, complemented by an adaptive probe-and-switch mechanism for low-noise regimes. Across the COCO bbob-noisy suite and external tasks including RL policy search and hyperparameter optimization, RB-PEM achieves consistent gains in high-misranking, budget-constrained settings.

### [186] [From Privacy to Workflow Integrity: Communication-Graph Metadata in Autonomous Agent Interoperability](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07150)
*Bijaya Dangol*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文揭示智能体通信协议(A2A/MCP)存在通信图元数据泄露问题：攻击者仅通过观察"谁连接谁、何时连接、频率如何"就能推断工作流状态和即将执行的动作。这种泄露不仅是隐私问题，更威胁工作流完整性——攻击者可在机器速度下利用预测性杠杆干扰自主行动。作者提出威胁模型，评估多种传输层方案，并通过A2A案例实验证明：仅凭被动元数据即可显著高于随机水平地识别任务类型，而采取的防护措施能有效将其压回随机水平。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能体互操作协议(A2A、MCP)标准化了智能体间的通信内容，并假设基于地址的HTTP(S)传输，虽然保护了消息内容（甚至端到端加密），但通信图（谁联系谁、何时、频率）完全暴露在明文之中。在智能体系统中，这种元数据泄露比传统隐私框架所暗示的更为严重——端点常带有能力标签，工作流具有结构化和链式特征，交互关联实际动作，因此观察者可以恢复的不只是历史关系，还能推断待进行的工作流、正在组装的任务以及即将执行的动作。更关键的是，这种推断可在机器速度下用于在工作流完成前采取行动，从而构成对工作流完整性的威胁，而非仅仅是隐私问题。

Method: 作者首先形式化了智能体通信图的威胁模型，识别了智能体元数据区别于传统元数据的三个关键特性：语义性（端点带有能力标签）、前瞻性（可推断未来动作）和致动性（关联实际物理/数字行动）。然后定义了传输层和引导层的隐私属性，评估了SimpleX/SMP、Tor、混合网络等候选传输方案。接着以A2A协议为案例研究，展示了元数据保护绑定可以在协议中表达但会暴露其身份假设。最后，基于真实A2A捕获数据构建生成模型进行实验验证：使用分类器从被动元数据（仅工作流开头部分）恢复任务类别，并测量防护属性对恢复率的抑制效果，以及攻击者利用泄露信息在固定预算下选择干扰目标所能获得的优势。

Result: 实验结果表明：仅从被动元数据（无任何负载内容），仅利用工作流开头部分，分类器即可显著高于随机水平地恢复任务类别。应用所提出的防护属性后，分类器的恢复能力被显著压制回接近随机水平。此外，在固定预算下，利用元数据泄露的对手可以获得接近"全知攻击者"相对于元数据盲攻击者的大部分优势，而同样的防护属性也能有效抑制这种优势。

Conclusion: 智能体通信中的元数据泄露不仅是隐私问题，更是工作流完整性的威胁。本文提出的威胁模型和防护属性为构建安全的智能体通信系统提供了理论基础。A2A案例研究表明现有协议的身份假设需要重新审视。未来的智能体通信设计应将元数据保护作为核心要求，而非事后补丁。

Abstract: Agent-interoperability protocols such as A2A and MCP standardize what agents say to one another, but assume address-based transport over HTTP(S). Such transports protect message content, increasingly with end-to-end encryption. What they leave in the clear is the communication graph: which agent contacts which, when, and how often. In agent systems this graph is more consequential than a privacy framing suggests. Endpoints are often capability-labeled, workflows are structured and chained, and interactions are coupled to real actions, so an observer recovers more than past relationships. It can infer the pending workflow, the task being assembled and the action likely to follow. At machine speed, it can act on that inference before the workflow completes. The threat is therefore one of workflow integrity, not privacy alone: predictive leverage over autonomous action. We give a threat model for the agent communication graph; identify what makes agent metadata distinctively revealing (semanticity, prospectivity, actuation); define transport- and bootstrap-layer privacy properties and weigh candidate transports (SimpleX/SMP, Tor, mixnets) against them; and present an A2A case study in which a metadata-protecting binding is expressible but surfaces the protocol's identity assumptions. We test these on a generative model anchored to a real A2A capture. From passive metadata alone, with no payloads, a classifier recovers a task's class well above chance, from only the workflow's opening; applied together, the properties drive that recovery sharply back toward chance. Beyond what an observer can recover, we measure the leverage of acting on the leak: from a workflow's opening and under a fixed budget, an adversary choosing which workflows to act on realizes in this model most of a clairvoyant attacker's advantage over a metadata-blind one, and the same properties suppress it.

</details>


### [187] [Rethinking IoT Intrusion Detection: Augmenting Routing Metrics with Radio Features](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07282)
*Yichang Sun,Andreas Johnsson,Sourasekhar Banerjee*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出在基于LSTM的入侵检测系统中，结合无线射频（TX/RX）特征与传统RPL路由层特征，以提升对RPL-based IoT网络的攻击检测性能。实验表明，该方法在DIS-Flooding、Local Repair和Worst Parent三种攻击下，F1分数最高提升约4%，对Worst Parent攻击效果最显著。

Result: 结合TX/RX特征后，F1分数相比仅使用路由层特征最高提升约4%，其中Worst Parent攻击的检测性能提升最为显著。

Abstract: Machine learning-based intrusion detection systems (IDS) for RPL-based IoT networks often rely solely on routing layer features, which provide only a partial view of network behaviour. In this work, we investigate whether incorporating Transmit (TX) and Receive (RX) radio features alongside the standard RPL feature set can improve detection performance in an LSTM-based IDS. We evaluate the proposed approach across three different attack types, namely DIS-Flooding, Local Repair, and Worst Parent under varying network sizes. The results show that incorporating TX and RX improves the IDS's overall detection performance by up to ~4% in F1-score compared with using routing-layer features alone, with the most notable gain observed for the Worst Parent attack.

### [188] [The Custody Envelope Threshold: Authority-Scaled Admission of External Artifacts in Institutional Infrastructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06767)
*Amadeus Brandes*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出"保管信封阈值"(Custody Envelope Threshold)框架，用于评估机构对外部制品的准入治理。当制品身份、入口路径和撤销能力相对于其执行权限不够封闭时，机构应采取代理、策略调解、内部化等措施。框架通过四条件有序工具操作化，并应用于多种现代基础设施制品。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代基础设施严重依赖外部维护的制品（如包依赖、CI/CD动作、容器镜像等），这些制品易于获取但难以被机构进行准入、治理和撤销，存在安全隐患。

Method: 提出了Custody Envelope Threshold框架，一个基于权限规模的制品准入模型。通过四条件有序工具（身份、入口路径、撤销能力、执行权限）评估制品的封闭性，并结合引用监控器推理、最小权限原则和交易成本经济学进行理论支持。

Result: 将框架应用于包依赖、GitHub Actions、容器镜像、Terraform提供者与模块、开发者扩展和开放模型制品。将MCP服务器作为保留证据进行验证。提供了验证设计、确定性预测函数和OSF复制包。

Conclusion: 高审查机构应趋向于对高权限制品实现更强保管封闭性。框架为机构治理外部制品提供了理论依据和可操作的工具。

Abstract: Modern infrastructure depends on externally maintained artifacts such as package-registry dependencies, CI/CD actions, container images, Terraform providers and modules, developer extensions, model artifacts, and AI tool servers. These artifacts are easy to fetch but difficult for institutions to admit, govern, and revoke. This paper proposes the Custody Envelope Threshold, an authority-scaled model of artifact admission. It argues that direct institutional admission is defensible only when object identity, ingress path, and revocation capacity are sufficiently closed relative to the execution authority delegated to the artifact. When this threshold is not met, institutions tend to proxy, policy-mediate, vendor-mediate, internalize, quarantine, or reject the artifact. The framework is operationalized as a four-condition ordinal instrument and connected to reference-monitor reasoning, least privilege, and transaction cost economics. It is applied to package dependencies, GitHub Actions, container images, Terraform providers and modules, developer extensions, and open model artifacts, with Model Context Protocol (MCP) servers treated as held-out evidence. The paper also specifies a validation design, deterministic prediction function, and OSF replication package for testing whether high-scrutiny institutions converge toward stronger custody closure for high-authority artifacts.

### [189] [MalSkillBench: A Runtime-Verified Benchmark of Malicious Agent Skills](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07131)
*Wenbo Guo,Wei Zeng,Chengwei Liu,Xiaojun Jia,Yijia Xu,Lei Tang,Yong Fang,Yang Liu*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 本文提出MalSkillBench——首个经过运行时验证的恶意AI agent技能基准测试，包含3,944个恶意技能样本，基于108维三维分类体系标注。研究发现：代码注入检测可达94.5%验证率但提示注入仅75.8%；最强技能检测器在代码注入上召回率98.4%，但在提示注入和agent控制攻击上完全失效；仅依赖野样本评估会使排名偏移高达66个召回点。现有供应链扫描器和提示注入防御均只能看到技能的一半，无法联合推理代码与指令的关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: AI编码agent（如Claude Code、Gemini CLI）正在通过第三方技能包扩展自身能力，这些技能同时包含自然语言指令、可执行脚本和工具权限，形成了既非纯代码也非纯提示的混合型供应链依赖。已有检测工具从未在这种混合空间上经过验证ground truth的评估，导致其有效性未知，且仅基于野生样本的评估存在偏差。

Method: 构建了MalSkillBench基准：1) 3,944个恶意技能，按108个单元的3维分类体系标注；2) 3,214个来自闭环生成-验证-反馈管道（Docker沙箱+系统调用监控+LLM裁判）；3) 补充703个野生样本和4,000个良性技能；4) 对多种检测器进行系统性评估。

Result: 代码注入验证率达94.5%，提示注入仅75.8%；野生样本高度偏倚（86.6%单一行为，81%来自两个账号）；最强技能检测器在代码注入上召回率98.4%，但在提示注入和agent控制攻击上完全崩溃；仅用野生样本评估会使排名偏移高达66个召回点；现有供应链扫描器和提示注入防御各只能覆盖技能的一半。

Conclusion: 检测恶意技能需要联合推理任务意图、代码和指令三者之间的关系，现有工具无法做到这一点。数据集、管道、基线和结果已开源发布。

Abstract: AI coding agents such as Claude Code and Gemini CLI increasingly extend themselves with third-party skills: markdown packages bundling natural-language instructions, executable scripts, and tool permissions. Because a skill is at once code and agent-facing instruction, it introduces a supply chain dependency whose risk is neither pure code nor pure prompt. Detection tools have never been measured against verified ground truth spanning this hybrid space, leaving their effectiveness unknown and wild-only evaluations biased.
  We present MalSkillBench, the first runtime-verified benchmark of malicious agent skills: 3,944 malicious skills labeled along a three-dimensional taxonomy of 108 cells. Of these, 3,214 come from a closed-loop Generate-Verify-Feedback pipeline admitting only samples whose malicious behavior fires inside a Docker sandbox under system-call monitoring and an LLM judge; we add 703 in-the-wild and 4,000 matched benign skills. Our measurements are consistent: code injection reaches 94.5% verification yield but prompt injection only 75.8%, the same fragility that later makes it hard to detect; the wild sample is narrow, dominated by one cryptocurrency-theft campaign (86.6% one behavior, 81% from two accounts) with a small but architecturally new tail attacking the agent control plane; the strongest skill-specific detector reaches 98.4% recall on code injection yet collapses on prompt-injection and agent-control attacks, and wild-only scoring swings the ranking by up to 66 recall points; supply-chain scanners and prompt-injection defenses each see only half of a skill, and no combination recovers the code-instruction relationship. Detecting malicious skills therefore requires reasoning jointly over task intent, code, and instructions. We release the dataset, pipeline, baselines, and results.

</details>


### [190] [On the Shoulders of Giants: Empowering Automated Smart Contract Auditing via the GiAnt Corpus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.07363)
*Xiaoting Zhang,Zhipeng Gao,Yiran Lv,Xing Hu,Feifei Niu,Xin Xia*

Main category: cs.CR

TL;DR: 提出GiANT框架，通过从Code4rena审计报告中提炼漏洞信息，自动构建高质量智能合约审计数据集GiAnt Corpus，包含7,711个漏洞发现，经人工评估质量得分4.76/5，并在多个任务上为LLM建立了性能基线。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有智能合约审计数据集存在两个主要局限：1) 人工构建导致扩展性瓶颈；2) 数据粒度和多样性不足。亟需自动化方法来构建高质量、大规模的数据集。

Method: GiANT采用分治策略结合思维链技术从Code4rena报告中提取结构化漏洞信息，再通过LLM-as-a-judge机制进行严格的质量保证。

Result: 在388份真实审计报告上运行，生成包含7,711个漏洞发现的GiAnt Corpus（跨5个严重等级）。人工评估质量得分4.76±0.37，评分者间一致性κ=0.88。在漏洞检测、代码摘要、缓解建议和gas优化任务上为4个SOTA LLM建立了基线。

Conclusion: GiANT框架有效解决了数据集的扩展性和粒度问题，生成的高质量数据集可为自动化智能合约审计研究提供有价值的数据基础。

Abstract: High-quality smart contract auditing datasets are crucial for evaluating security tools and advancing smart contract security research. Two major limitations of existing datasets are the manual-induced scalability bottleneck and the deficiency in data granularity and diversity. To address these limitations, we propose GiANT, an automated framework designed to curate smart contract auditing datasets by distilling vulnerability insights from real-world auditing reports. GiANT employs a divide-and-conquer strategy coupled with the Chain-of-Thought technique to extract structured vulnerability information from Code4rena reports, followed by an LLM-as-a-judge mechanism to perform rigorous quality assurance. To evaluate GiANT's effectiveness, we run it on 388 real-world audit reports and generate the GiAnt Corpus comprising 7,711 vulnerability findings across five severity levels. Manual assessment of the dataset demonstrates exceptional reliability in information extraction, achieving a mean quality score of $4.76\pm0.37$ (out of 5) with inter-rater agreement $κ$ of 0.88. We further validate the practicality of our dataset by benchmarking 4 state-of-the-art LLMs on vulnerability detection, code summarization, mitigation recommendation, and automated gas optimization tasks, to establish performance baselines, thereby providing a valuable data foundation for future research in automated smart contract auditing.

</details>

### [192] [AI Level of Detail: Distance-Aware ML Model Precision Selection for Real-Time Human Motion Prediction in Games](https://arxiv.org/abs/2606.06565)
*Mathew Varghese*

Main category: cs.GR

TL;DR: 本文提出 AI LOD 框架，根据 NPC 与玩家相机的距离动态调整机器学习推理精度（FP32、FP16、INT8），在远距离使用低精度模型以节省算力，且感知质量下降可忽略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现代游戏引擎在 NPC 动画的机器学习推理上消耗大量计算资源，而传统几何 LOD 已证明远距离可使用低精度近似。作者希望将类似思路推广到 AI 推理层面，在感知不敏感的场景下用低精度模型替代高精度模型以节省计算。

Method: 借鉴几何 LOD 思想，提出 AI LOD 框架：将训练好的运动模型导出为 FP32、FP16、INT8 三种 ONNX Runtime 变体，运行时根据 NPC 到玩家相机的距离选择对应精度版本进行推理。使用 Li 等人的卷积序列到序列模型作为代表性示例，在 CMU Mocap 数据集上评估。

Result: 在 CMU Mocap 数据集上的初步评估表明，每个精度层级在分配的距离范围内均可正常服务，且感知退化程度可忽略不计。

Conclusion: 距离感知的 ML 模型精度选择是 AI 驱动角色动画中可行的 LOD 策略，且该概念可推广到任何感知敏感性随上下文变化的 AI 运行时系统。

Abstract: Modern game engines spend significant compute animating NPCs with learned motion models. This paper proposes AI Level of Detail (AI LOD), a framework in which machine learning inference precision is adapted based on the distance between each NPC and the player camera. The core idea mirrors classical geometry LOD: substitute a cheaper approximation where the difference is imperceptible. Here, the approximation is a lower-precision quantized machine learning model rather than a lower-polygon mesh.
  The contribution of this work is the AI LOD concept itself: that inference-time quantization can serve as the LOD axis for AI-driven character animation - and more broadly, for any AI-based runtime system where perceptual sensitivity varies with context. The convolutional sequence-to-sequence model of Li et al. is used as a representative example to demonstrate the concept, with its trained checkpoint exported into three ONNX Runtime variants (FP32, FP16, and INT8 per-tensor), intended to be routed by a distance-based selector at runtime. Evaluation on the CMU Mocap dataset provides initial evidence that each precision tier can be served at its assigned distance range with negligible perceptible degradation, supporting the broader premise that distance-aware ML model precision selection is a viable LOD strategy for AI-based character animation.

</details>
